					Read More
				</span> <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mdc-icon mds-icon mdc-button__content mdc-button__icon mds-button__icon mds-button__icon--right" data-v-7322780e=""><use xlink:href="/assets/img/mds.3ec6f34.svg#caret-down"></use></svg></button></div></div></label> <div id="mds-accordion-transparency-drawer" class="mdc-grid mds-layout-grid mds-accordion__content" data-v-bcc0c73a=""><div class="mdc-row mds-layout-grid__row" data-v-18387644="" data-v-bcc0c73a=""><div class="mdc-column mds-layout-grid__col mds-layout-grid__col--12 mds-layout-grid__col--6-at-768 mds-layout-grid__col--3-at-1092" data-v-7ba8d775="" data-v-18387644=""><div class="mdc-transparency-drawer__main-description" data-v-7ba8d775=""><p>Transparency is how we protect the integrity of our work and keep empowering investors to achieve their goals and dreams. And we have unwavering standards for how we keep that integrity intact, from our research and data to our policies on content and your personal data. </p>
<p>We’d like to share more about how we work and what drives our day-to-day business.</p></div></div> <div class="mdc-column mds-layout-grid__col mds-layout-grid__col--12 mds-layout-grid__col--6-at-768 mds-layout-grid__col--9-at-1092" data-v-7ba8d775="" data-v-18387644=""><div class="mdc-grid mds-layout-grid" data-v-bcc0c73a="" data-v-7ba8d775=""><div class="mdc-row mds-layout-grid__row mdc-transparency-drawer__accordions-container" data-v-18387644="" data-v-bcc0c73a=""><div class="mdc-column mds-layout-grid__col mds-layout-grid__col--12 mds-layout-grid__col--4-at-1092" data-v-7ba8d775="" data-v-18387644=""><div aria-labelledby="transparency-drawer-accordion-1--title" class="mds-module-container" data-v-7ba8d775=""><div class="mds-accordion mdc-transparency-drawer__secondary-accordion" data-v-7ba8d775=""><input id="transparency-drawer-accordion-1" type="checkbox" aria-controls="mds-accordion-transparency-drawer--1" class="mds-accordion__trigger" data-v-7ba8d775=""> <label for="transparency-drawer-accordion-1" class="mds-accordion__label" data-v-7ba8d775=""><img src="https://images.contentstack.io/v3/assets/blt4eb669caa7dc65b2/blt3bce7cffbeb60a42/60809fdf26fd84453c018424/make-money.svg" alt="" class="mdc-image" data-v-7ba8d775="" width="85px" height="64px"> <div id="transparency-drawer-accordion-1--title" class="mdc-header mds-header mds-header--level-5 mds-header--primary mds-header--border-bottom" data-v-6968a9be="" data-v-7ba8d775=""><h3 class="mdc-header__title mds-header__title" data-v-6968a9be="">
											How we make money
										</h3> <!----></div></label> <section id="mds-accordion-transparency-drawer--1" class="mds-accordion__content" data-v-7ba8d775=""><p>We sell different types of products and services to both investment professionals and individual investors. These products and services are usually sold through license agreements or subscriptions. Our investment management business generates asset-based fees, which are calculated as a percentage of assets under management. We also sell both admissions and sponsorship packages for our investment conferences and advertising on our websites and newsletters. <br></p>
<p></p></section></div></div></div> <div class="mdc-column mds-layout-grid__col mds-layout-grid__col--12 mds-layout-grid__col--4-at-1092" data-v-7ba8d775="" data-v-18387644=""><div aria-labelledby="transparency-drawer-accordion-2--title" class="mds-module-container" data-v-7ba8d775=""><div class="mds-accordion mdc-transparency-drawer__secondary-accordion" data-v-7ba8d775=""><input id="transparency-drawer-accordion-2" type="checkbox" aria-controls="mds-accordion-transparency-drawer--2" class="mds-accordion__trigger" data-v-7ba8d775=""> <label for="transparency-drawer-accordion-2" class="mds-accordion__label" data-v-7ba8d775=""><img src="https://images.contentstack.io/v3/assets/blt4eb669caa7dc65b2/blt218bb7805fb32c9a/60809fdfb35a7a3c69a379ff/personal-data.svg" alt="" class="mdc-image" data-v-7ba8d775="" width="85px" height="64px"> <div id="transparency-drawer-accordion-2--title" class="mdc-header mds-header mds-header--level-5 mds-header--primary mds-header--border-bottom" data-v-6968a9be="" data-v-7ba8d775=""><h3 class="mdc-header__title mds-header__title" data-v-6968a9be="">
											How we use your personal data
										</h3> <!----></div></label> <section id="mds-accordion-transparency-drawer--2" class="mds-accordion__content" data-v-7ba8d775=""><p>How we use your information depends on the product and service that you use and your relationship with us. We may use it to:</p><ul><li>Verify your identity, personalize the content you receive, or create and administer your account.</li><li>Provide specific products and services to you, such as portfolio management or data aggregation.</li><li>Develop and improve features of our offerings.</li><li>Gear advertisements and other marketing efforts towards your interests.</li></ul>
<p>To learn more about how we handle and protect your data, visit our <a href="/company/privacy-center">privacy center</a>.</p></section></div></div></div> <div class="mdc-column mds-layout-grid__col mds-layout-grid__col--12 mds-layout-grid__col--4-at-1092" data-v-7ba8d775="" data-v-18387644=""><div aria-labelledby="transparency-drawer-accordion-3--title" class="mds-module-container" data-v-7ba8d775=""><div class="mds-accordion mdc-transparency-drawer__secondary-accordion" data-v-7ba8d775=""><input id="transparency-drawer-accordion-3" type="checkbox" aria-controls="mds-accordion-transparency-drawer--3" class="mds-accordion__trigger" data-v-7ba8d775=""> <label for="transparency-drawer-accordion-3" class="mds-accordion__label" data-v-7ba8d775=""><img src="https://images.contentstack.io/v3/assets/blt4eb669caa7dc65b2/blta8bf8e458b569f88/60809fdf03ce953dac756a01/editorial-content.svg" alt="" class="mdc-image" data-v-7ba8d775="" width="85px" height="64px"> <div id="transparency-drawer-accordion-3--title" class="mdc-header mds-header mds-header--level-5 mds-header--primary mds-header--border-bottom" data-v-6968a9be="" data-v-7ba8d775=""><h3 class="mdc-header__title mds-header__title" data-v-6968a9be="">
											How we approach editorial content
										</h3> <!----></div></label> <section id="mds-accordion-transparency-drawer--3" class="mds-accordion__content" data-v-7ba8d775=""><p>Maintaining independence and editorial freedom is essential to our mission of empowering investor success. We provide a platform for our authors to report on investments fairly, accurately, and from the investor’s point of view. We also respect individual opinions––they represent the unvarnished thinking of our people and exacting analysis of our research processes. Our authors can publish views that we may or may not agree with, but they show their work, distinguish facts from opinions, and make sure their analysis is clear and in no way misleading or deceptive.</p>
<p>To further protect the integrity of our editorial content, we keep a strict separation between our sales teams and authors to remove any pressure or influence on our analyses and research.</p>
<p>Read our <a href="/editorial-policy">editorial policy</a> to learn more about our process.</p></section></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></aside></div> <footer
